		var tempObj = {

			'sku': el.sku,

			'price': el.price,

			'quantity': el.quantity

	});

	})

  <script>_satellite["_runScript5"](function(event, target, Promise) {

function fixArr(arr) {

    if (typeof (arr) === "object" && arr[0] && arr[0].skuId) {

        return arr;

    }



    if (typeof (arr) === undefined) {

        return null;

    }

    var temporalArr = [];

    if (Array.isArray(arr)) {

        temporalArr = arr;

    }

    if (typeof (arr) === "string") {

        temporalArr = arr.split(",");

    }



    var fixedArray = []

    temporalArr.forEach(function(el) {

        fixedArray.push({

            "skuId": el

        });

    });

    return fixedArray;



}



function fetchProductUpdatedInfo(skuString, callback) {



    //XMLHttpRequest

    var skuObj = fixArr(skuString);

    if (skuObj) {

        var fetchItemDetailRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();

        var fetchItemDetailURL = "/s/browse/v1/fetchItemDetails/co?" + encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify({

            "products": skuObj

        }));



        fetchItemDetailRequest.addEventListener('load', function(event) {



                var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText);

                if (response.success && response.success === true) {

                    var filteredProducts = response.products.map(function(el) {

                        if (el.product.published !== false && el.product.purchasable !== false) {



                            var tempEl = {};

                            tempEl.id = el.product.id;

                            tempEl.prices = el.product.prices;

                            tempEl.prices.forEach(function(el2) {

                                el2.price = el2.originalPrice||el2.formattedLowestPrice;

                                delete el2.originalPrice;

                                delete el2.label;

                                delete el2.isLoyalty;

                                delete el2.opportunidadUnica;

                                delete el2.symbol;



                            });

                            return tempEl;



                        }

                    });

                  if(callback){

                       callback(filteredProducts);

                  }else{

                    console.log(filteredProducts);

                  }





                }



                if (response.success && response.success === false && callback) {

                     callback(null);



                }

        });



        fetchItemDetailRequest.open("GET", fetchItemDetailURL, true);

        fetchItemDetailRequest.send();

    }

}



window.fetchProductUpdatedInfo=fetchProductUpdatedInfo;

});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript6"](function(event, target, Promise) {

var searchSelector = 'input[class*="SearchBar"]';

var resultAreaSelector = 'div[class*="SearchList-module_searchResults"]';

var sessionStorageName = 'typeaheadresult';



function handleEvent(el) {



    var sectionText;

    var section = el.closest('section');



    var greenResult;

    var pickedElementText = el.innerText;



    var searchTerm = document.querySelector(searchSelector);





    try {

        sectionText = section.querySelector('h6').innerText

    } catch (e) {

        sectionText = 'keyword';

        greenResult = 'en negro';

    }



    var options = section.querySelector('ul').childNodes;



    var index = getIndex(el, options);



    /**

     * When index is Not a Number, the result is inside green section

     */

    if (isNaN(index)) {

        options.forEach(function(e) {

            var ul = e.querySelector('ul');

            if (ul) {

                pickedElementText = ul.parentNode.querySelector('a').innerText;

                options = ul.childNodes;

                index = getIndex(el, options);

                greenResult = 'en verde';

            }

        });

    }

    sessionStorage.setItem(sessionStorageName,

        searchTerm.value + '|' + sectionText + '|' + pickedElementText + '|' + index + '/' + options.length + (greenResult ? '|' + greenResult : '')

    );

}



function getIndex(element, list) {

    var index;

    list.forEach(function(e, i) {

        if (e.querySelector('a').href == element.href) {

            index = i;

        }

    });

    return index + 1;

}





function execute() {

    try {

        var current = 0,

            tries = 10;

        var resultArea;



        var interval = setInterval(function() {



            resultArea = document.querySelector(resultAreaSelector);



            if (resultArea) {

                var links = resultArea.querySelectorAll('a');



                links.forEach(function(l) {

                    l.addEventListener('click', function() {

                        handleEvent(l);

                    });

                });

                clearInterval(interval);

            }





            if (tries < current) {

                clearInterval(interval);

            }



            current++;

        }, 500);

    } catch (ex) {}

}





document.addEventListener('click', function() {

    execute();

});



var inputBar = document.querySelector('#testId-SearchBar-Input');

if (inputBar) {

    inputBar.addEventListener('change', function() {

        execute();

    });

}

});</script>

const getParent = () => {

  const parentSelectors = [

    "div#main-Banner-8a41851a-d8d8-4e8c-9fba-a249afc45899",

    "div#main-Banner-69b195a9-c50a-457b-a428-efedd368de94",

    "div#main-PowercardCarousel-aeb29e00-5e7d-4dbe-9f48-0d136f681ad4"

  ];



  for (let x = 0; x < parentSelectors.length; x++) {

    const parent = document.querySelector(parentSelectors[x]);

    if (parent) {

      return parent;

    }

  }

};



const getSiS = () => {

  const s = window.location.host;

  if (s.startsWith("homecenter.")) {

    return "homecenter";

  } else if (s.startsWith("sodimac.")) {

    return "sodimac";

  } else if (s.startsWith("linio.")) {

    return "linio";

  } else if (s.startsWith("tienda.")) {

    return "tienda";

  } else if (s.startsWith("tottus.")) {

    return "tottus";

  }

  return null;

};



const getTag = (sis) => {

  let tag = "F.com";

  if (sis === "tottus") {

    tag = "Tottus";

  } else if (sis === "linio") {

    tag = "Linio";

  } else if (sis === "tienda") {

    tag = "FRetail";

  } else if (sis === "sodimac") {

    tag = "Sodimac";

  } else if (sis === "homecenter") {

    tag = "Homecenter";

  }



  return {

    tag: `Recs!Home!CO_${tag}!Rec_1!x!Populares`,

    dataWrapper: `C-Home_${tag}-REC1-Populares`,

  };

};



const appendTemplate = (id) => {

  const container = document.createElement("div");

  container.id = "flb-carousel-exp-" + id;

  container.innerHTML = getTemplate(id);



  //changeSelector

  const parent = getParent();



  if (!parent) {

    return false;

  }



  parent.appendChild(container);

  return true;

};



const addCarouselScript = () => {

  const head = document.querySelector("head");

  const previousScript = document.querySelector('script[src="' + jsCar + '"]');

  if (head && !previousScript) {

    const carrScript = document.createElement("script");

    document.querySelector("head").appendChild(carrScript);

    carrScript.src = jsCar;

  }

};



const initCarousel = (id, sku) => {

  const carousel = document.querySelector(`#${id}`);

  if (carousel) {

    const sis = getSiS();

    const tag = getTag(sis);

    const intervalID = setInterval(() => {

      if (carousel.init) {

        carousel.init({

          title: "Productos más populares",

          ...tag,

          productPageSku: sku,

          inHouseConfig: {

            widgetsUUID: "653cf655-5224-4cac-a247-f61a786dc174",

            pageType: "HOME",

          },

        });

        clearInterval(intervalID);

      }

    }, 500);

  }

};



(() => {

  const id = "home-retorno-rec1";

  const parentExists = appendTemplate(id);



  if (parentExists) {

    addCarouselScript();

    initCarousel(id, "home");

  }

})();



});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript20"](function(event, target, Promise) {

/**

 * EXP-53

/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element anchor element

 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain

 */

function isOutOfDomain(element) {

    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {

            return false;

        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {

            return true;

        }

        return true;

    }

    return false;

}



var ui = {

    isSLP: function() {

        return true;

    },

    str: function str() {

        return 'T|x|x|x|x|x|x|x|x';



    },

    approvedTrackClick: function approvedTrackClick(menulink) {

        var isMenuLink = false;

        if (/(ThirdLevelItems|SecondLevelItems|ToggleThirdCategories|thirdLevelMenu)/.test(menulink.className) || menulink && menulink.parentElement && /secondLevelMenu__/.test(menulink.parentElement.className) || menulink.closest('[class*="thirdLevelMenu__mobile"]')) {

            isMenuLink = true;

        }

        if (!isMenuLink)

            return;

        var finalCondition = false;

        finalCondition = isMenuLink;

        return finalCondition;

    },

    firstLevelDescription: function() {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');

            menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

            var a = menuItemsArr.find(function(element, i) {

                if (/active/.test(element.className)) {

                    return element;

                }

            });

            return windowW ? document.querySelector('[class*="firstLevelMenu__title--active"]').textContent.trim() : a.textContent.trim();

        } else {

            return windowW ? document.querySelector("#mobile-item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim() : document.querySelector("#item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim();

        }

    },

    firstLevelPosition: function() {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024,

            index, menuItems;

        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            if (windowW) {

                index = false;

                menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__title"]');

                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {

                    if (/--active/.test(element.className)) {

                        index = i;

                    }

                });

                return index;

            } else {

                index = false;

                menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');

                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {

                    if (/active/.test(element.className)) {

                        index = i;

                    }

                });

                return index;

            }

        } else {

            index = false;

            var section = window.screen.width < 1024 ? document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] section") : document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] > div > section");

            section = Array.from(section);

            section.map(function(element, i) {

                if (/display/.test(element.className)) {

                    index = i;

                }

            });



            return index;

        }

    },

    secondLevelDescription: function(theParent) {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;



        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            if (windowW) {

                return (theParent.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]') || theParent.closest('ul[class=""]').querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')).querySelector('a').textContent.trim();

            } else {

                return theParent.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]').textContent.trim();

            }



        } else {

            if (windowW) {

                return theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]') ? theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]').querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim() : theParent.closest('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel]').previousSibling.querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim()

            } else {

                return theParent.querySelector('[class*="SecondLevelItems_submenuTitle"]').textContent.trim();



            }

        }

    },

    order: function order(el, type) {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024,

            thirdLevelContainer, thirdLevelLinkArr, clickedThirdLevel;

        var order = false;

        var menuLink = el;



        var columnOrder = function() {

            return windowW ? menuLink.closest("nav").querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu"]') : menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenuContainer"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu__dekstop"]');

        };

        columnOrder = [].slice.apply(columnOrder());



        if (windowW && type === "column") {

            var newMenuLink = menuLink.closest("ul:not([class])");

            var newMenuLinkArr = [].slice.apply(newMenuLink.querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]'));

            return (newMenuLinkArr.indexOf(menuLink.closest('ul[class=""]').querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')) + 1);



        }

        //desktop

        if (!windowW && type === "column") {

            return (columnOrder.indexOf(menuLink.closest('ul[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')) + 1);

        }



        //mobile

        if (windowW && type === "row") {

            if (menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]')) {

                return 0;

            } else {

                thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('[class*="thirdLevelMenu__mobile"]');

                thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));

                clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');

                return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;



            }

        }



        if (!windowW && type === "row") {



            if (menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]')) {

                return 0;

            } else {

                thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('ul[class*="thirdLevelMenu"]');

                thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));

                clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');

                return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;



            }

        }

        var filterColum = function() {

            if (ui.isSLP()) {

                if (windowW) {

                    var a = columnOrder.find(function(el) {

                        if (el.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title--active"]')) {

                            return el.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title--active"]');

                        }

                    });

                    return [].slice.apply(a.querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]'));

                } else {

                    return columnOrder;

                }

            } else {

                return columnOrder;

            }

        };

        filterColum().map(function(el, i) {

            var rgx = el.textContent;



            var title = function() {

                if (ui.isSLP()) {

                    return el.innerText.split("\n", 1)[0];

                } else {

                    return el.textContent.substr(0, secondLevelDescription.length);

                }

            };



            var theParent = function() {

                if (windowW) {

                    return linkTo;

                } else {

                    if (menuLink.className.indexOf("thirdLevelMenu--link") > -1 || menuLink.className.indexOf("ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLi") > -1) {

                        return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement

                    } else {

                        return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;

                    }

                }

            };

            var secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());



            if (title() === secondLevelDescription) {



                if (rgx.indexOf(menuLink.textContent.trim()) > -1) {

                    var indexColumn = i;

                    var thisSlpTitle = ui.isSLP() ? /__title/.test(menuLink.className) : /_submenuTitle/.test(menuLink.className);

                    if (thisSlpTitle) {

                        if (menuLink.textContent === el.querySelector('[class*="_submenuTitle"]').textContent) {

                            switch (type) {

                                case "column":

                                    order = indexColumn;

                                    break;

                                case "row":

                                    order = /<\/a>/.test(menuLink.outerHTML) ? indexColumn = 0 : indexColumn + 1;

                                    break;

                                default:

                                    break;

                            }

                        }

                    } else {

                        var isSLPListElement = ui.isSLP() ? el.querySelectorAll('li') : el.querySelectorAll("[class*=ThirdLevelItems_listElements]");

                        // var thirdLink = windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                        var thirdLink = function() {

                            if (ui.isSLP()) {

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"] [class*="secondLevelMenu__content"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                            } else {

                                // return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuMobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel] li') : isSLPListElement;

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="activeMobileThirdLevel"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems]') : isSLPListElement;

                            }

                        };

                        thirdLink = [].slice.apply(thirdLink());

                        thirdLink.map(function(el, i) {

                            if (el.textContent.trim() === menuLink.textContent.trim()) {

                                switch (type) {

                                    case "column":

                                        order = indexColumn;

                                        break;

                                    case "row":

                                        order = ui.isSLP() ? i - 1 : i + 1;

                                        break;

                                    default:

                                        break;

                                }

                            }

                        });

                    }

                }

            }

        });

        return order;

    }

};



function execute() {



    var firstLevelDescription, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition,

        columnOrder, rowOrder, firstLevelCollection, linksCollection, columnCollection;



    var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

    var topLevelMenu = document.querySelector('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') ? document.querySelectorAll('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') : document.querySelectorAll('.fb-masthead__new-hamburger-menu [class*="_firstCategories"],[class*="CategoryMenuButton-module_menu-toggle-button"]');

    //var validateServer = digitalData.page.serverName;

    if (topLevelMenu.length === 0)

        return;

    document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {

        try {

            var menuLink = windowW ? event.target : event.target.closest('a');

            var anchorLink = menuLink ? menuLink.closest('a') || menuLink.querySelector('a') : null;



            if (menuLink && ui.approvedTrackClick(menuLink)) {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition() + 1;

                firstLevelDescription = ui.firstLevelDescription();

                var linkTo = event.target || event.target.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.querySelector('[class*="submenuTitleToggleActive"]');

                var theParent = function() {

                    if (windowW) {

                        return linkTo;

                    } else {

                        if (menuLink.className.indexOf("thirdLevelMenu--link") > -1 || menuLink.className.indexOf("ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLi") > -1) {

                            return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement

                        } else {

                            return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;

                        }

                    }

                };

                secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());

                thirdLevelDescription = menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "" && menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "arrow" ? menuLink.textContent.trim() : secondLevelDescription;



                columnOrder = ui.order(menuLink, 'column');

                rowOrder = ui.order(menuLink, 'row') === -1 ? 0 : ui.order(menuLink, 'row');



                if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                    localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                    //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                }



                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



            }

            if (/img_banner/.test(event.target.className)) {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition();

                var topCategory = event.target.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.closest('[class*="submenuStage"]').querySelector('[class*="FirstLevelItems_menuElementsHover"]').textContent;

                if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                    localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                }

                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', topCategory + '|' + 'B1' + '|' + ImgName + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + '50' + '|' + '1');

            }

            if (event.target.closest('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_category-content-container"],[class*="CategoryMenuMobile-module_mobile-menu-container"]')) {

                if (window.screen.width < 1024) {

                    //dosomething

                    if (event.target.closest('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]') || event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category"]') && event.target.localName !== "svg" && !/CategoryMenuButton-module_hamburger/i.test(event.target.className)) {

                        columnCollection = [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[data-testid="first-level-category"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]'));

                        linksCollection = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]') ? [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="MenuBody-module_leaf-category-item"]')) : [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]').parentElement.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[class*="MenuBody-module_leaf-category-item"]'));

                        firstLevelCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-1"]'));

                        linksCollection = [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]'));

                        firstLevelCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid="desktop-menu-category-button"]'))



                        firstLevelPosition = firstLevelCollection.indexOf(document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"]')) + 1;

                        firstLevelDescription = document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"] span').innerText;

                        columnOrder = columnCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('ul'));

                        secondLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('ul').querySelector('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        thirdLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        rowOrder = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? 0 : linksCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]')) + 1;

                        if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                            localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                            //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                        }

                        localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



                    }



                }

            }

            if (menuLink && windowW && !ui.approvedTrackClick(menuLink) && (menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'))) {



                var listElement = menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]');

                var menuItems = Array.from(listElement.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'));

                var menuDescription = listElement.innerText.trim().replace(/\r?\n|\r/g, ' ');

                menuDescription = menuDescription.startsWith('Tienes') ? 'Mis CMR puntos' : menuDescription;



                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + 'H' + (menuItems.indexOf(listElement) + 1) + '|0|0');

            }



            if (_satellite && localStorage.getItem('topLevelMenuCoords') && isOutOfDomain(anchorLink)) {

                _satellite.track('OOD_CALL');

            }

        } catch (ex) {}

    });

}



execute();

});</script>

var UI = (function() {

  function UI() {

    _classCallCheck(this, UI);

  }



  _createClass(UI, [

    {

      key: "findStyleTag",

      value: function findStyleTag(where, what) {

        var a = document.getElementsByTagName(where)[0].children;

        a = Array.from(a);

        var styleTags = a.filter(function(el) {

          return el.localName === what;

        });

        return styleTags[0];

      }

    },

    {

      key: "createTag",

      value: function createTag(name, content) {

        //return `<meta name="${name}" content="${content}">`

        var meta = document.createElement("meta");

        meta.name = name;

        meta.content = content;

        return meta;

      }

    }

  ]);



  return UI;

})();



//init function



function addMetas() {

  var ui = new UI();

  var firstStyle = ui.findStyleTag("head", "style");



  metaInfo.map(function(el) {

    var tags = ui.createTag(el.name, el.content);

    firstStyle.insertAdjacentElement("beforebegin", tags);

  });

}

addMetas();

function valid(name) {

  // TODO: validate against options dictionary

  return name.indexOf('smartbanner:') !== -1 && name.split(':')[1].length > 0;

}



function convertToCamelCase(name) {

  var parts = name.split('-');

  parts.map(function (part, index) {

    if (index > 0) {

      parts[index] = part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.substring(1);

    }

  });

  return parts.join('');

}



var OptionParser = function () {

  function OptionParser() {

    _classCallCheck(this, OptionParser);

  }



  _createClass(OptionParser, [{

    key: 'parse',

    value: function parse() {

      var metas = document.getElementsByTagName('meta');

      var options = {};

      var optionName = null;

      Array.from(metas).forEach(function (meta) {

        var name = meta.getAttribute('name');

        var content = meta.getAttribute('content');

        if (name && content && valid(name) && content.length > 0) {

          optionName = name.split(':')[1];

          if (Array.from(optionName).includes('-')) {

            optionName = convertToCamelCase(optionName);

          }

          options[optionName] = content;

        }

      });

      return options;

    }

  }]);



  return OptionParser;

}();



exports.default = OptionParser;

  originalTop: 'data-smartbanner-original-top',

  originalMarginTop: 'data-smartbanner-original-margin-top'

};



function handleExitClick(event, self) {

  self.exit();

  event.preventDefault();

}



function handleJQueryMobilePageLoad(event) {

  if (!this.positioningDisabled) {

    setContentPosition(event.data.height);

  }

}



function addEventListeners(self) {

  var closeIcon = document.querySelector('.js_smartbanner__exit');

  closeIcon.addEventListener('click', function (event) {

    return handleExitClick(event, self);

  });

  if (_detector2.default.jQueryMobilePage()) {

    $(document).on('pagebeforeshow', self, handleJQueryMobilePageLoad);

  }

}



function removeEventListeners() {

  if (_detector2.default.jQueryMobilePage()) {

    $(document).off('pagebeforeshow', handleJQueryMobilePageLoad);

  }

}



function setContentPosition(value) {

  var wrappers = _detector2.default.wrapperElement();

  for (var i = 0, l = wrappers.length, wrapper; i < l; i++) {

    wrapper = wrappers[i];

    if (_detector2.default.jQueryMobilePage()) {

      if (wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalTop)) {

        continue;

      }

      var top = parseFloat(getComputedStyle(wrapper).top);

      wrapper.setAttribute(datas.originalTop, isNaN(top) ? 0 : top);

      wrapper.style.top = value + 'px';

    } else {

      if (wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalMarginTop)) {

        continue;

      }

      var margin = parseFloat(getComputedStyle(wrapper).marginTop);

      wrapper.setAttribute(datas.originalMarginTop, isNaN(margin) ? 0 : margin);

      //wrapper.style.marginTop = value + 'px';

    }

  }

}



function restoreContentPosition() {

  var wrappers = _detector2.default.wrapperElement();

  for (var i = 0, l = wrappers.length, wrapper; i < l; i++) {

    wrapper = wrappers[i];

    if (_detector2.default.jQueryMobilePage() && wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalTop)) {

      wrapper.style.top = wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalTop) + 'px';

    } else if (wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalMarginTop)) {

      wrapper.style.marginTop = wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalMarginTop) + 'px';

    }

  }

}



var SmartBanner = function () {

  function SmartBanner() {

    _classCallCheck(this, SmartBanner);



    var parser = new _optionparser2.default();

    this.options = parser.parse();

    this.platform = _detector2.default.platform();

  }



  // DEPRECATED. Will be removed.





  _createClass(SmartBanner, [{

    key: 'publish',

    value: function publish() {

      if (Object.keys(this.options).length === 0) {

        throw new Error('No options detected. Please consult documentation.');

      }



      if (_bakery2.default.baked) {

        return false;

      }



      // User Agent was explicetely excluded by defined excludeUserAgentRegex

      if (this.userAgentExcluded) {

        return false;

      }



      // User agent was neither included by platformEnabled,

      // nor by defined includeUserAgentRegex

      if (!(this.platformEnabled || this.userAgentIncluded)) {

        return false;

      }



      var siteWrapper = document.querySelector(".site-wrapper");

      var bannerDiv = document.createElement('div');

      siteWrapper.insertAdjacentElement('beforebegin', bannerDiv);

      //document.querySelector('body').appendChild(bannerDiv);

      bannerDiv.outerHTML = this.html;

      if (!this.positioningDisabled) {

        setContentPosition(this.height);

      }

      addEventListeners(this);

    }

  }, {

    key: 'exit',

    value: function exit() {

      removeEventListeners();

      if (!this.positioningDisabled) {

        restoreContentPosition();

      }

      var banner = document.querySelector('.js_smartbanner');

      document.querySelector('body').removeChild(banner);

      _bakery2.default.bake(this.hideTtl, this.hidePath);

    }

  }, {

    key: 'originalTop',

    get: function get() {

      var wrapper = _detector2.default.wrapperElement()[0];

      return parseFloat(wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalTop));

    }



    // DEPRECATED. Will be removed.



  }, {

    key: 'originalTopMargin',

    get: function get() {

      var wrapper = _detector2.default.wrapperElement()[0];

      return parseFloat(wrapper.getAttribute(datas.originalMarginTop));

    }

  }, {

    key: 'priceSuffix',

    get: function get() {

      if (this.platform === 'ios') {

        return this.options.priceSuffixApple;

      } else if (this.platform === 'android') {

        return this.options.priceSuffixGoogle;

      }

      return '';

    }

  }, {

    key: 'icon',

    get: function get() {

      if (this.platform === 'android') {

        return this.options.iconGoogle;

      } else {

        return this.options.iconApple;

      }

    }

  }, {

    key: 'buttonUrl',

    get: function get() {

      if (this.platform === 'android') {

        return this.options.buttonUrlGoogle;

      } else if (this.platform === 'ios') {

        return this.options.buttonUrlApple;

      }

      return '#';

    }

  }, {

    key: 'html',

    get: function get() {

      var modifier = !this.options.customDesignModifier ? this.platform : this.options.customDesignModifier;

      return '<div class="smartbanner smartbanner--' + modifier + ' js_smartbanner">\n      <a href="javascript:void();" class="smartbanner__exit js_smartbanner__exit"></a>\n      <div class="smartbanner__icon" style="background-image: url(' + this.icon + ');"></div>\n      <div class="smartbanner__info">\n        <div>\n          <div class="smartbanner__info__title">' + this.options.title + '</div>\n          <div class="smartbanner__info__author">' + this.options.author + '</div>\n </div>\n      </div>\n      <a href="' + this.buttonUrl + '" target="_blank" class="smartbanner__button"><span class="smartbanner__button__label">' + this.options.button + '</span></a>\n    </div>';

      //<div class="smartbanner__info__price">' + this.options.price + this.priceSuffix + '</div>\n 

    }

  }, {

    key: 'height',

    get: function get() {

      var height = document.querySelector('.js_smartbanner').offsetHeight;

      return height !== undefined ? height : 0;

    }

  }, {

    key: 'platformEnabled',

    get: function get() {

      var enabledPlatforms = this.options.enabledPlatforms || DEFAULT_PLATFORMS;

      return enabledPlatforms && enabledPlatforms.replace(/\s+/g, '').split(',').indexOf(this.platform) !== -1;

    }

  }, {

    key: 'positioningDisabled',

    get: function get() {

      return this.options.disablePositioning === 'true';

    }

  }, {

    key: 'userAgentExcluded',

    get: function get() {

      if (!this.options.excludeUserAgentRegex) {

        return false;

      }

      return _detector2.default.userAgentMatchesRegex(this.options.excludeUserAgentRegex);

    }

  }, {

    key: 'userAgentIncluded',

    get: function get() {

      if (!this.options.includeUserAgentRegex) {

        return false;

      }

      return _detector2.default.userAgentMatchesRegex(this.options.includeUserAgentRegex);

    }

  }, {

    key: 'hideTtl',

    get: function get() {

      return this.options.hideTtl ? parseInt(this.options.hideTtl) : false;

    }

  }]);



  console.log("connected");

  return SmartBanner;

}();





exports.default = SmartBanner;
